The door was locked and I opened the door immediately to remove the disinfectant paper towels. The result was Neither of the two room key cards could open the door, and even when the waiter came to clean the room, the special room card couldn't be opened. The supervisor also came, but fortunately the supervisor warded off evil spirits and opened the door.
The hotel breakfast was too expensive for a room price of more than 800 yuan, so I just changed places after just one bite. I also placed an order at the Greater China Hilton on Ctrip and asked for a special car to move to the Hilton.
The Zhongzhou Shengtingyuan Hotel looked good from the outside in the morning, but after checking in, I realized that it was a "strong on the outside but poor on the inside" with dilapidated hardware and insufficient shower water pressure.
But the hygiene of the hotel room was okay, and the waiters and room attendants I met were all good.
It is very convenient to live here when visiting "Huaqiangbei". You can go shopping and look at electronic products, but mainly wholesale.

msg:挺好的，位置好，在地鐵3號線新華站C出口旁邊10米的地方就是酒店大堂，鬧中取靜，房間也很安靜，不吵。房間裏有很多細節值得表揚，花灑下面有個可以放沐浴露的小架子，拿取沐浴露和洗髮水很方便，不要小看這個架子，很多酒店都沒有，沖涼的時候，用沐浴露和洗髮水的時候很不方便，衹能放在地上，非常的不科學和不方便。衞生間洗手枱的右下方有紙巾使用和拿取非常方便隨手。房間裏有賺送蘋果，雪梨和香蕉各一個，很新鮮，味道很不錯，這個贈送水果在其他的酒店比較少有。從酒店大堂出去步行約十分鐘左右的地方有麥當勞和購物廣場，吃飯購物都很方便。
